                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">حَسُنَ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">حسن</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">حسنن</orth>
                  </form>, (S, Mgh, Msb, K, &amp;c.,) which may also be written and pronounced <foreign lang="ar">حَسْنَ</foreign>, with the dammeh suppressed, (S,) and <foreign lang="ar">حَسَنَ</foreign>, (K,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">حَسُنَ</orth>
                  </form>, (TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">حُسْنٌ</foreign> (S, * Msb, K, * TA) and <foreign lang="ar">حُسْنَى</foreign>, (Ham p. 657, and Bd in ii. 77,) <hi rend="ital">He,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it</hi> (a thing, S, Msb), <hi rend="ital">had,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">possessed, the quality termed</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">حَسْنٌ</foreign> [which see below; i. e., <hi rend="ital">was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, good,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">goodly,</hi> (generally the latter,) <hi rend="ital">beautiful, comely,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">pleasing,</hi> &amp;c.; and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8000-1" target="تحسّن" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n8004"/></foreign> often signifies the same, as in the phrase <foreign lang="ar">تحسّن عِنْدَهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">it was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, good,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">in his estimation</hi>]: (S, K, TA:) and [in like manner] <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8000-2" target="أَحْسَنَ" n="2" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>زَيْدٌ</foreign> means <hi rend="ital">Zeyd became possessed of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">حُسْن</foreign>. (Mughnee in art. <foreign lang="ar">بِ</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  One may not say <foreign lang="ar">حُسْنَ</foreign>, transferring the dammeh of the <foreign lang="ar">س</foreign> to the <foreign lang="ar">ح</foreign> and making the former letter quiescent, except in one case; because it is [virtually, together with its agent expressed or implied, in this case,] a predicate: [see I'Ak p. 234:] this is allowable only in the case of a verb of praise or dispraise; <foreign lang="ar">حُسْنَ</foreign>, in respect of the transference of the medial vowel, being likened to <foreign lang="ar">نِعْمَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">بِئْسَ</foreign>, which are originally <foreign lang="ar">نَعِمَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">بَئِسَ</foreign>: and thus one does in all verbs like these two in meaning: a poet says, <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">لَمْ يَمْنَعِ النَّاسُ مِنِّى مَا أَرَدْتُ وَ مَا</foreign>
                     </L> 
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">أُعْطِيهِمُ مَا أَرَادُوا حُسْنَ ذَا أَدَبَا</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> 
                  <hi rend="ital">[Men have not withheld from me what I have desired, nor do I give them what they have desired: good,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">very good, is this as a mode of conduct!</hi>]: meaning <foreign lang="ar">حَسُنَ هٰذَا أَدَبًا</foreign>. (S, TA.) You say also, <foreign lang="ar">حَسُنَ زَيْدٌ</foreign>, [meaning <hi rend="ital">Good,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">goodly,</hi> &amp;c., or <hi rend="ital">very good</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">is Zeyd!</hi> or] meaning <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8000-3" target="أَحْسِنْ" n="3" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>بِهِ</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">how good,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">goodly,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">is Zeyd!</hi> as also   
      <foreign lang="ar">مَا <ref cref="n8000-4" target="أَحْسَنَهُ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>]. (B, TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">بِ</foreign>.)    </entryFree>26:T81a,<entryFree id="n8001" key="حسّنهُ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>2</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">حسّنهُ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">حسن</orth>

                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">حسننه</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">حسنة</orth>
                  </form>, (S, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَحْسِينٌ</foreign>, (S,) <hi rend="ital">He made it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">rendered it,</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">حَسَن</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">good,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">goodly,</hi> (generally the latter,) <hi rend="ital">beautiful, comely,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">pleasing,</hi> &amp;c.]; (K;) <hi rend="ital">he beautified, embellished,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">adorned, it;</hi> (S, TA;) as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8001-1" target="احسنهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>. (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8001-2" target="أَحْسَنَ" n="2" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>الحَلَّاقُ رَأْسَهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The shaver beautified,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">trimmed, his head.</hi> (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">الَّذِى  <ref cref="n8001-3" target="أَحْسَنَ" n="3" type="6" subtype="FTFSO" lang="ar"/> كُلَّ شَىْءٍ خَلَقَهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Who hath made good,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">goodly, everything that He hath created</hi>], in the Kur [xxxii. 6], means <foreign lang="ar">حَسَّنَ خَلْقَ كُلِّ شَىْءٍ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">hath made good,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">goodly, the creation of everything</hi>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [See also <foreign lang="ar">تَحْسِينٌ</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And see 10.    </entryFree>27:T1530,<entryFree id="n8003" key="احسن" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>4</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">احسن</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">احسن</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">أحسن</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">أحسنن</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">حسن</orth>
                  </form> as an intrans. v.: see 1.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">He did that which was</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">حَسَن</foreign> [meaning <hi rend="ital">good, comely,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">pleasing; he acted well</hi>]; (Msb;) <hi rend="ital">he did a good deed:</hi> (Er-Rághib, TA:) [for] <foreign lang="ar">إِحْسَانٌ</foreign> is the <hi rend="ital">contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">إِسَآءَةٌ</foreign>: (K:) it differs from <foreign lang="ar">إِنْعَامٌ</foreign> in being to oneself and to another; whereas the latter is only to another: (TA:) and it surpasses <foreign lang="ar">عَدْلٌ</foreign>, inasmuch as it means the <hi rend="ital">giving more than one owes,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">taking less than is owed to one;</hi> whereas the latter means the giving what one owes, and taking what is owed to one. (Er-Rághib, TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">أَحْسَنْتُ إِلَيْهِ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">بِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I acted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">behaved, with goodness, well,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">in a good</hi> or <hi rend="ital">comely</hi> or <hi rend="ital">pleasing manner, towards him; did good to him; benefited him; conferred a benefit,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">benefits, upon him</hi>]: both signify the same: (S, TA:) and hence, in the Kur [xii. 101], <foreign lang="ar">قَدْ أَحْسَنَ بِى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">إِذَ أَخْرَجَنِى مِنَ السِّجْنِ</foreign> meaning <foreign lang="ar">إِلَىَّ</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">He hath acted well towards me, when he brought me forth from the prison</hi>]: (AHeyth, Az:) or, accord. to some, the verb in this case is made to import the meaning of <foreign lang="ar">لَطَفَ</foreign> [which is trans. by means of <foreign lang="ar">بِ</foreign>, i. e. <hi rend="ital">He hath acted graciously with me</hi>]. (Mughnee in art. <foreign lang="ar">بِ</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">الإِحْسَانُ</foreign> is also explained as meaning <foreign lang="ar">الإِخْلَاصُ</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">The being sincere,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">without hypocrisy;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the asserting oneself to be clear of believing in any beside God</hi>]; which is a condition of the soundness, or validity, of <foreign lang="ar">الإِيمَان</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">الإِسْلَام</foreign> together: and as denoting <hi rend="ital">watchfulness, and good obedience:</hi> and as meaning <hi rend="ital">the continuing in the right way, and following the way which those [of the righteous] who have gone before have trodden;</hi> this last being said to be the meaning in the Kur ix. 101.                   </form>, fem. <foreign lang="ar">حَسْنَآءُ</foreign>, pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَحَاسِنُ</foreign>: see <foreign lang="ar">حَسَنٌ</foreign>.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">الأَحْسَنُ</foreign> denotes the comparative and superlative degrees [of <foreign lang="ar">حُسْنٌ</foreign>]; as in the phrase <foreign lang="ar">هُوَ الأَحْسَنُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, is the better,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">best;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the more,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">most, goodly</hi> or <hi rend="ital">beautiful</hi> or <hi rend="ital">comely</hi> &amp;c.]: (K:)   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8022-1" target="الحُسْنَى" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> is the fem.; as in the phrase <foreign lang="ar">الأَسْمَآءُ الحُسْنَى</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The best names;</hi> those of God; which are ninety and nine: (Jel in vii. 179:) it signifies <hi rend="ital">the contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">السُّوْءَى</foreign>: (S, K:) the pl. of <foreign lang="ar">الأَحْسَنُ</foreign> is <foreign lang="ar">الأَحَاسِنُ</foreign>. (K.) In the saying, in the Kur [vi. 153 and xvii. 36], <foreign lang="ar">وَ لَا تَقْرَبُوا مَالَ اليَتِيمِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">إِلَّا بِالَّتِى هِىَ أَحْسَنُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And approach ye not the property of the orphan,</hi> to make use of it,] <hi rend="ital">except by that</hi> act <hi rend="ital">which is best</hi> to be done with it, the meaning is, such an act as the taking care of it, and increasing it: (Bd:) or, as some say, the meaning is, the taking, of his property, what will [suffice to] conceal those parts of one's person that should not be exposed, and stay one's hunger. (TA.) [The fem.]   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8022-2" target="الحُسْنَى" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> is applied to accidents only: not to substances. (Er-Rághib, TA.) It means also, [as an epithet in which the quality of a subst. predominates, <hi rend="ital">That which is better,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">that which is best.</hi> And hence,] <hi rend="ital">The good final</hi> or <hi rend="ital">ultimate state</hi> or <hi rend="ital">condition</hi> [appointed for the faithful]: (K:) so, it is said, in the Kur xli. 50. (TA.) And <hi rend="ital">The view,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">vision, of God;</hi> (K;) accord. to some: but it is said that in the Kur x. 27, it means <hi rend="ital">Paradise;</hi> and <foreign lang="ar">زِيَادَةٌ</foreign>, which there follows it, means the view, or vision, of the face of God. (TA.) And <hi rend="ital">Victory:</hi> and <hi rend="ital">martyrdom:</hi> (Th, K:) whence, [in the Kur ix. 52,] <foreign lang="ar">إِحْدَى</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الحُسْنَيَيْنِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">one of the two best things</hi>]; (K;) <hi rend="ital">victory or martyrdom.</hi> (Ksh, Bd, Jel.) And <hi rend="ital">The saying</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">لَا إِلَاهَ إِلَّا ٱللّٰهُ</foreign>. (Jel in xcii. 6 and 9.) The pl. of   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8022-3" target="الحُسْنَى" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> is <foreign lang="ar">الحُسْنَيَاتُ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n8022-4" target="الحُسَنُ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n8009"/></foreign>, (K, [the latter like <foreign lang="ar">رُجَعٌ</foreign> pl. of <foreign lang="ar">رُجْعَى</foreign>, but misunderstood by Freytag as syn. with <foreign lang="ar">المَحَاسِنُ</foreign>, which next follows it in the K,]) neither of which is used without the article <foreign lang="ar">ال</foreign>. (TA.)    </entryFree>2f:T4c7,<entryFree id="n8024" key="تَحْسِينٌ" type="main">
